beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'fau', 0, 0
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(19)
      debugLogForScript: s32'20', 0, 0
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg7), Val(0)
      findState: s32'cmn_AfroObj', 11, 2, 52
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 800
          setObjectHeight: 800
          setObjectDepth: 800
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(20)
      debugLogForScript: s32'160', 0, 0
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 1000
          setObjectHeight: 1000
          setObjectDepth: 1000
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'uni'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'uni', 0, 0
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  isObjectActive: (STACK0)
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    if: Mem(IsMainPlayerSelf)
      createObject: s32'QH_MASTER', (PLAYER)
      stackObject: (STACK0), (PREVIOUS)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  isObjectActive: (STACK2)
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    if: Mem(PlayerVal1)
      createObject: s32'QH_MONITOR_eff', (PLAYER)
      stackObject: (STACK2), (PREVIOUS)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'sol'

beginState: s32'CmnActMatchWin'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnactmatchwin'
    cinesco: 1
    swapMeshSet: s32'800cs'
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'macthwin_enemycheck', Val(0), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg7), Val(800)
      playAnimation: s32'luc800cs', 0
      checkLastStateName: s32'WinActionWait'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        playCameraAnimation: s32'luc800cs', 23, 0, -1
      endIf: 
      else: 
        playCameraAnimation: s32'luc800cs', 23, 17, -1
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg7), Val(810)
      playAnimation: s32'luc810cs', 0
      checkLastStateName: s32'WinActionWait'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        playCameraAnimation: s32'luc810cs', 23, 0, -1
      endIf: 
      else: 
        playCameraAnimation: s32'luc810cs', 23, 17, -1
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 263
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(7)
